WT3_Travel.c(174):     function daysInAdvanceDiscountLevel(ticketDate) {\n
WT3_Travel.c(174):       today = new Date()\n
WT3_Travel.c(174):       msPerDay = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000\n
WT3_Travel.c(174):       DIA = (ticketDate.getTime() - today.getTime()) / msPerDay + 1\n
WT3_Travel.c(174):       DIA = Math.floor(DIA)\n
WT3_Travel.c(174):     \n
WT3_Travel.c(174):       return DIA \n
WT3_Travel.c(174):     }\n
WT3_Travel.c(174):     \n
